<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">berôven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">birōvon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*biraubōną</i>; equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roven.html>roven</a></i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:berusten.html>berusten</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rusten.html>rusten</a></i>.
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to resign oneself, to be resigned [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> <span>(object)</span></span> = to], to accept after resisting; settle for

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschieten.html>beschieten</a> (17700)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschieten.html>beschieten</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schieten.html>schieten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschieten.html>beschieten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shoot at, to fire at
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:smokkelaars.html>smokkelaars</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werden.html>werden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beschoten.html>beschoten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijlen.html>pijlen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">People <b>shot</b> arrows at the smugglers.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brabant" class="extiw" title="w:Brabant">Brabant</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make progress with; to benefit or thrive from; to suffice</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Holland" class="extiw" title="w:Holland">Holland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to nap, to doze</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschikken.html>beschikken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschikking.html>beschikking</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschikkingen.html>beschikkingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschikking.html>beschikkinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>power of control, direction or disposal; decision, ruling <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">by an authorized official or official body such as a court</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>; mastery, <span class="Latn" lang="en">command</span> <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<span id="rfv-sense-notice-nl-"></span>Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> verify<sup class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=Wiktionary:Requests_for_verification/Non-Englishamp;action=editamp;section=newamp;preload=Template:rfv-sense/preloadamp;preloadtitle=%5B%5Bbeschikking%23rfv-sense-notice-nl-%7cbeschikking%5D%5D">+</a>)</sup> this sense?)</span>

***beschouwen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschouwen.html>beschouwen</a> (6276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschouwen.html>beschouwen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schouwen.html>schouwen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschouwen.html>beschouwen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to contemplate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to consider, to regard [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span> = as]</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">consider</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opvatten.html>opvatten</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitleggen.html>uitleggen</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:beschouwen.html>beschouwen</a></b>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bescrivinge</i>. ***beschuit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschuit.html>beschuit</a> (44079)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">biscuit</i>, plausibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">bescuit</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twice cooked</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Old Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">biscotto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">biscoctum</i>, from Latin <i>(panis) bis coctus</i> "(bread) twice-baked."
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschuldigen.html>beschuldigen</a></i>, replacing older <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">beschulden</i> by influence of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schuldich</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuldig.html>schuldig</a></i>). ***beseffen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beseffen.html>beseffen</a> (4712)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beseffen.html>beseffen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*biseffen</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bi-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*seffen</i>. The latter part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sabjaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beseffen.html>beseffen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to realize</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beseffen.html>Beseffen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not reflexive, but occasionally it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> wrongly used reflexively: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beseffen.html>beseffen</a></i>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> probably a contamination of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:realiseren.html>realiseren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to realize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the same meaning, but reflexive.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

***beslaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beslaan.html>beslaan</a> (42551)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">beslaen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beslaan.html>beslaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover, occupy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Noord-Brabant <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beslaat.html>beslaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebied.html>gebied</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> 4919 <a href = vnd.unilang:vierkant.html>vierkante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kilometer.html>kilometer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">North Brabant <b><a href = vnd.unilang:covers.html>covers</a></b> an area of 4919 square <a href = vnd.unilang:kilometers.html>kilometers</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to surround, <a href = vnd.unilang:envelop.html>envelop</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fog up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruiten.html>ruiten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:besloegen.html>besloegen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:waardoor.html>waardoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>windows</a> <b>fogged up</b> so that I could not see anything anymore.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shoe (a horse with horseshoes)</li></ol>

***beslag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beslag.html>beslag</a> (12491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">beslach</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beslag.html>beslag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beslagen.html>beslagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beslag.html>beslagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> arrest, detention
<dl><dd><i>in <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beslag.html>beslag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a></i>: to take into possession, to confiscate</dd></dl></li>
<li>(metal) cover (e.g. of a book)</li>
<li>a horseshoe</li>
<li>a <span class="Latn" lang="en">batter</span>, a relatively fluid dough <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">more fluid than <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deeg.html>deeg</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>the state of having reached the final decision or having definitively decided upon an arrangement</li></ol>

<ul><li><i>(horseshoe)</i> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoefijzer.html>hoefijzer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoefbeslag</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:besluiten.html>besluiten</a> (6738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">besluten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bislūtan</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sluiten.html>sluiten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:besluiten.html>besluiten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decide, to make a decision</li></ol>

***besmeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:besmeren.html>besmeren</a> (95300)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:besmeren.html>besmeren</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smeren.html>smeren</a></i>. A variant Hollandic form <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> rise to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:besmeuren.html>besmeuren</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:besmeren.html>besmeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grease, to dirty, to apply grease or dirt to</li></ol>
